114
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Legislative Assembly and Offices</h1>
115
      
116
    </div>
117
    <div class="row">
118
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
119
      <div xml:lang="en">
120
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
121
          Government of Ontario : Legislative Assembly and Offices</h3>
122
        <p>This category includes the disclosures of Ministers, MPPs and Legislative Offices.</p>
123
      </div>
124
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
125
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
126

127
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe les ministres, les d&eacute;put&eacute;s et bureaux l&eacute;gislatifs.</p>

  <div id="right_column">
20673
    <div class="row clearfix">
20674
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Ministries</h1>
20675
      
20676
    </div>
20677
    <div class="row">
20678
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
20679
      <div xml:lang="en">
20680
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
20681
          Government of Ontario : Ministries</h3>
20682
        <p>This category includes all ministries.</p>
20683
      </div>
20684
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
20685
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
20686
          Gouvernement de l&rsquo;Ontario : Minist&egrave;res</h3>
20687
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe tous les minist&egrave;res.</p>
20688
      </div>
20689
      <table border="0" width="100%"  cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" summary="Salary Disclosure">
20690
        <thead>
20691
          <tr>
20692

38901
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Ministries</h1>
38902
      
38903
    </div>
38904
    <div class="row">
38905
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
38906
      <div xml:lang="en">
38907
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
38908
          Government of Ontario : Ministries</h3>
38909

      </div>

    <div class="row clearfix">
57141
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Ministries</h1>
57142
      
57143
    </div>
57144
    <div class="row">
57145
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
57146
      <div xml:lang="en">
57147
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
57148
          Government of Ontario : Ministries</h3>
57149
        <p>This category includes all ministries.</p>
57150
      </div>
57151
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
57152
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
57153
          Gouvernement de l&rsquo;Ontario : Minist&egrave;res</h3>
57154
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe tous les minist&egrave;res.</p>
57155
      </div>

    <div class="row clearfix">
75384
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Ministries</h1>
75385
      
75386
    </div>
75387
    <div class="row">
75388
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
75389
      <div xml:lang="en">
75390
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
75391
          Government of Ontario : Ministries</h3>
75392
        <p>This category includes all ministries.</p>
75393
      </div>
75394
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
75395
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
75396
          Gouvernement de l&rsquo;Ontario : Minist&egrave;res</h3>
75397
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe tous les minist&egrave;res.</p>
75398
      </div>

93669
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Ministries</h1>
93670
      
93671
    </div>
93672
    <div class="row">
93673
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
93674
      <div xml:lang="en">
93675
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
93676
          Government of Ontario : Ministries</h3>
93677

93678
      </div>

98240
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Colleges</h1>
98241
      
98242
    </div>
98243
    <div class="row">
98244
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
98245
      <div xml:lang="en">
98246
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
98247
          Colleges</h3>
98248
        <p>This category includes Ontario Colleges.</p>
98249
      </div>
98250
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
98251

98252
          Coll&egrave;ges</h3>
98253
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les coll&egrave;ges de l'Ontario.</p>

    <div class="row clearfix">
116478
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Colleges</h1>
116479
      
116480
    </div>
116481
    <div class="row">
116482
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
116483
      <div xml:lang="en">
116484
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
116485
          Colleges</h3>
116486
        <p>This category includes Ontario Colleges.</p>
116487
      </div>
116488
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
116489
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
116490
          Coll&egrave;ges</h3>
116491
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les coll&egrave;ges de l'Ontario.</p>
116492
      </div>

      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Colleges</h1>
134756
      
134757
    </div>
134758
    <div class="row">
134759
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>

136742
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Other Public Sector Employers</h1>
136743
      
136744
    </div>
136745
    <div class="row">
136746
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
136747
      <div xml:lang="en">
136748
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
136749
          Other Public Sector Employers</h3>
136750
        <p>This category includes all other organizations and corporations not captured in a specific category.</p>
136751
      </div>
136752
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
136753
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
136754
          Autres employeurs du secteur public</h3>
136755
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe toutes les organisations et soci&eacute;t&eacute;s qui n'entrent pas dans une cat&eacute;gorie en particulier.</p>
136756
      </div>

    <div class="row clearfix">
154984
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Other Public Sector Employers</h1>
154985
      
154986
    </div>
154987
    <div class="row">
154988
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
154989
      <div xml:lang="en">
154990
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
154991
          Other Public Sector Employers</h3>
154992
        <p>This category includes all other organizations and corporations not captured in a specific category.</p>
154993
      </div>
154994
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
154995
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
154996
          Autres employeurs du secteur public</h3>
154997
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe toutes les organisations et soci&eacute;t&eacute;s qui n'entrent pas dans une cat&eacute;gorie en particulier.</p>
154998
      </div>

173236
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Other Public Sector Employers</h1>
173237
      
173238
    </div>
173239
    <div class="row">
173240
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
173241
      <div xml:lang="en">
173242
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
173243
          Other Public Sector Employers</h3>
173244
        <p>This category includes all other organizations and corporations not captured in a specific category.</p>
173245
      </div>
173246
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">

175323
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h1>
175324
      
175325
    </div>
175326
    <div class="row">
175327
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
175328
      <div xml:lang="en">
175329
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
175330
          Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h3>
175331
        <p>This category includes Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. and their subsidiaries.</p>
175332
      </div>
175333
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
175334
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
175335
          Hydro One et Ontario Power Generation </h3>
175336
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. et leurs filiales.</p>
175337
      </div>

    <div class="row">
193554
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
193555
      <div xml:lang="en">
193556
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
193557
          Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h3>
193558
        <p>This category includes Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. and their subsidiaries.</p>
193559
      </div>
193560
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
193561

193562
          Hydro One et Ontario Power Generation </h3>
193563
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. et leurs filiales.</p>

    <div class="row clearfix">
211786
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h1>
211787
      
211788
    </div>
211789
    <div class="row">
211790
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
211791
      <div xml:lang="en">
211792
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
211793
          Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h3>
211794
        <p>This category includes Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. and their subsidiaries.</p>
211795
      </div>
211796
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
211797
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
211798
          Hydro One et Ontario Power Generation </h3>
211799
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. et leurs filiales.</p>
211800
      </div>

230032
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h1>
230033
      
230034
    </div>
230035
    <div class="row">
230036
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
230037
      <div xml:lang="en">
230038
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
230039
          Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h3>
230040
        <p>This category includes Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. and their subsidiaries.</p>
230041
      </div>
230042
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
230043
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
230044
          Hydro One et Ontario Power Generation </h3>
230045
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. et leurs filiales.</p>

266505
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h1>
266506
      
266507
    </div>
266508
    <div class="row">
266509
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
266510
      <div xml:lang="en">
266511
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
266512
          Hydro One and Ontario Power Generation</h3>
266513
        <p>This category includes Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. and their subsidiaries.</p>
266514
      </div>
266515
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
266516
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
266517
          Hydro One et Ontario Power Generation </h3>
266518
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie englobe Hydro One Inc., Ontario Power Generation Inc. et leurs filiales.</p>

</div><a href="/en/">Home</a> > <a href="/en/publications/salarydisclosure/pssd/">Salary Disclosure</a> > Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</div>

282717
<!-- end #header div -->  <a name="top" id="top"></a> <a name="main"></a>

  <div id="right_column">
282719
    <div class="row clearfix">
282720
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h1>
282721
      
282722
    </div>
282723
    <div class="row">
282724
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
282725
      <div xml:lang="en">
282726
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
282727
          Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h3>
282728
        <p>This category includes Ontario Hospitals and Boards of Public Health. Some Boards of Public Health can be found under a municipality in the "Municipalities and Services" category.</p>
282729
      </div>
282730
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
282731
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
282732
          H&ocirc;pitaux et Conseils de sant&eacute; </h3>
282733
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les h&ocirc;pitaux de l'Ontario et les Conseils de sant&eacute;. Il se peut que certains Conseils de sant&eacute; soient inclus dans la divulgation d'une municipalit&eacute; dans la cat&eacute;gorie "Municipalit&eacute;s et services".</p>
282734
      </div>

		_h.appendChild(_s);
300842
	})();
300843
} catch(e){}
300844
/*]]>*/
300845
</script>
300846

300847
<!-- end Footer --></div>
300848
<!-- END PAGE WRAPPER --> 
300849

300967
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h1>
300968
      
300969
    </div>
300970
    <div class="row">
300971
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
300972
      <div xml:lang="en">
300973
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
300974
          Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h3>
300975
        <p>This category includes Ontario Hospitals and Boards of Public Health. Some Boards of Public Health can be found under a municipality in the "Municipalities and Services" category.</p>
300976
      </div>
300977
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
300978
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
300979
          H&ocirc;pitaux et Conseils de sant&eacute; </h3>
300980
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les h&ocirc;pitaux de l'Ontario et les Conseils de sant&eacute;. Il se peut que certains Conseils de sant&eacute; soient inclus dans la divulgation d'une municipalit&eacute; dans la cat&eacute;gorie "Municipalit&eacute;s et services".</p>
300981
      </div>

  <div id="right_column">
319203
    <div class="row clearfix">
319204
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h1>
319205
      
319206
    </div>
319207
    <div class="row">
319208
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
319209
      <div xml:lang="en">
319210
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
319211
          Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h3>
319212
        <p>This category includes Ontario Hospitals and Boards of Public Health. Some Boards of Public Health can be found under a municipality in the "Municipalities and Services" category.</p>
319213
      </div>
319214
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
319215
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
319216
          H&ocirc;pitaux et Conseils de sant&eacute; </h3>
319217
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les h&ocirc;pitaux de l'Ontario et les Conseils de sant&eacute;. Il se peut que certains Conseils de sant&eacute; soient inclus dans la divulgation d'une municipalit&eacute; dans la cat&eacute;gorie "Municipalit&eacute;s et services".</p>
319218
      </div>

337454
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h1>
337455
      
337456
    </div>
337457
    <div class="row">
337458
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
337459
      <div xml:lang="en">
337460
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
337461
          Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h3>
337462
        <p>This category includes Ontario Hospitals and Boards of Public Health. Some Boards of Public Health can be found under a municipality in the "Municipalities and Services" category.</p>
337463
      </div>
337464
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
337465
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
337466
          H&ocirc;pitaux et Conseils de sant&eacute; </h3>
337467
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les h&ocirc;pitaux de l'Ontario et les Conseils de sant&eacute;. Il se peut que certains Conseils de sant&eacute; soient inclus dans la divulgation d'une municipalit&eacute; dans la cat&eacute;gorie "Municipalit&eacute;s et services".</p>
337468
      </div>

    <div class="row clearfix">
355689
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h1>
355690
      
355691
    </div>
355692
    <div class="row">
355693
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
355694
      <div xml:lang="en">
355695
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
355696
          Hospitals and Boards of Public Health</h3>
355697
        <p>This category includes Ontario Hospitals and Boards of Public Health. Some Boards of Public Health can be found under a municipality in the "Municipalities and Services" category.</p>
355698
      </div>
355699
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
355700
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
355701
          H&ocirc;pitaux et Conseils de sant&eacute; </h3>
355702
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les h&ocirc;pitaux de l'Ontario et les Conseils de sant&eacute;. Il se peut que certains Conseils de sant&eacute; soient inclus dans la divulgation d'une municipalit&eacute; dans la cat&eacute;gorie "Municipalit&eacute;s et services".</p>
355703
      </div>

367634
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
367635
      
367636
    </div>
367637
    <div class="row">
367638
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
367639
      <div xml:lang="en">
367640
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
367641
          Universities </h3>
367642
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
367643
      </div>
367644
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
367645
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
367646
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
367647
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>
367648
      </div>

  <div id="right_column">
385872
    <div class="row clearfix">
385873
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
385874
      
385875
    </div>
385876
    <div class="row">
385877
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
385878
      <div xml:lang="en">
385879
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
385880
          Universities </h3>
385881
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
385882
      </div>
385883
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
385884
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
385885
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
385886
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>
385887
      </div>
385888
      <table border="0" width="100%"  cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" summary="Salary Disclosure">
385889
        <thead>
385890
          <tr>
385891
            <td align="left" valign="top"><a href="/en/publications/salarydisclosure/pssd/orgs.php?pageNum_pssd=0&totalRows_pssd=15583&organization=universities&amp;year=2013">First&nbsp;page</a></td>
385892
            <td align="left" valign="top"><a href="/en/publications/salarydisclosure/pssd/orgs.php?pageNum_pssd=0&totalRows_pssd=15583&organization=universities&amp;year=2013">Previous</a></td>
385893

404113
    <div class="row clearfix">
404114
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
404115
      
404116
    </div>
404117
    <div class="row">
404118
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
404119
      <div xml:lang="en">
404120
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
404121
          Universities </h3>
404122
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
404123
      </div>
404124
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
404125
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
404126
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
404127
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>
404128
      </div>

    <div class="row clearfix">
422372
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
422373
      
422374
    </div>
422375
    <div class="row">
422376
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
422377
      <div xml:lang="en">
422378
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
422379
          Universities </h3>
422380
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
422381
      </div>
422382
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
422383
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
422384
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
422385
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>
422386
      </div>
422387
      <table border="0" width="100%"  cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" summary="Salary Disclosure">

440640
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
440641
      
440642
    </div>
440643
    <div class="row">
440644
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
440645
      <div xml:lang="en">
440646
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
440647
          Universities </h3>
440648
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
440649
      </div>
440650
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
440651

440652
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
440653
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>

      </div>

458872
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
458873
      
458874
    </div>
458875
    <div class="row">
458876
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
458877
      <div xml:lang="en">
458878
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
458879
          Universities </h3>
458880
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
458881
      </div>
458882
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
458883
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
458884
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
458885
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>

477101
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
477102
      
477103
    </div>
477104
    <div class="row">
477105
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
477106
      <div xml:lang="en">
477107
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
477108
          Universities </h3>
477109
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
477110
      </div>
477111
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
477112
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
477113
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
477114
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>

      </div>

495328
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Universities </h1>
495329
      
495330
    </div>
495331
    <div class="row">
495332
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
495333
      <div xml:lang="en">
495334
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
495335
          Universities </h3>
495336
        <p>This category includes Ontario Universities as well as colleges affiliated with universities.</p>
495337
      </div>
495338
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
495339
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
495340
          Universit&eacute;s </h3>
495341
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les universit&eacute;s de l'Ontario ainsi que leurs coll&egrave;ges affili&eacute;s.</p>
495342
      </div>

509803
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Crown Agencies</h1>
509804
      
509805
    </div>
509806
    <div class="row">
509807
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
509808
      <div xml:lang="en">
509809
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
509810
          Crown Agencies</h3>
509811
        <p>This category includes agencies, boards and commissions established by the government.</p>
509812
      </div>
509813
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
509814
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
509815
          Organismes de la Couronne </h3>
509816
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les organismes, conseils et commissions &eacute;tablis par le gouvernement.</p>
509817
      </div>

528053
    <div class="row clearfix">
528054
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Crown Agencies</h1>
528055
      
528056
    </div>
528057
    <div class="row">
528058
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
528059
      <div xml:lang="en">
528060
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
528061
          Crown Agencies</h3>
528062
        <p>This category includes agencies, boards and commissions established by the government.</p>
528063
      </div>
528064
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
528065
        <h3>Divulgation pour 2013 en vertu de la Loi de 1996 sur la divulgation des traitements dans le secteur public <br />
528066
          Organismes de la Couronne </h3>
528067
        <p>Cette cat&eacute;gorie contient les organismes, conseils et commissions &eacute;tablis par le gouvernement.</p>
528068
      </div>

541027
      <h1> Public Sector Salary Disclosure for 2013: Government of Ontario : Judiciary</h1>
541028
      
541029
    </div>
541030
    <div class="row">
541031
      <p><strong>The information contained in these pages is a copy of the official documents of these organizations.  Since the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act does not specify the language in which these documents need to be prepared, the Ministry of Finance publishes these documents in the original language in which they were prepared and presented to the Ministry. </strong></p>
541032
      <div xml:lang="en">
541033
        <h3>Disclosure for 2013 under the Public Sector Salary Disclosure Act, 1996<br />
541034
          Government of Ontario : Judiciary</h3>
541035
        <p>This category includes the Ontario Court of Justice and the Superior Court of Justice.</p>
541036
      </div>
541037
      <div xml:lang="fr-ca">
